      (conv3): BaseConv(
        (conv): Conv2d(512, 512, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (bn): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=0.001, momentum=0.03, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        (act): SiLU(inplace=True)
      )
      (m): Sequential(

          (conv1): BaseConv(

    )
  )
